msg:This is far from a 5 star hotel. Primarily, the hotel is dated and old, even though it indicated it was renovated (bathroom - yes, and some wall make up). The carpet in the room was absolutely disgusting, not just from being stained, but full of hair and crumbs. The bathroom towels had hair, as well as everywhere else. The breakfast was ok, enough variety for all. Dining area was full of flies though. Note that the hotel did not accept credit cards.

posted:Posted December 23, 2023
msg:Nice hotel stay.
However, I want to complain about this meal!
Went for dinner in the evening. A discount of 20 yuan per person brings the price down to 88 yuan. There is barbecue, drinks, hot dishes, cooked noodles, etc. When it comes to barbecue, it's just a grilled dragon fish, with bones and flesh attached. Speaking of hot dishes, no hot dish can make people even slightly satisfied. It said mutton soup, but it said mutton soup, but there was no mutton soup. It only asked you to order mutton soup, and you ordered a little mutton soup and a bunch of vermicelli. Okay, I'll put less vermicelli next time, but it works. There is only a small amount of haggis in a bowl of soup, and the haggis is so fat that it makes people sigh. Eat a cake. There are only one or two varieties of ready-made cakes. If you eat one at random, it will be tasteless. Finally? ! There is a small hot pot, let's cook some vegetables and eat them. The enoki mushrooms are a bit dry. By the way, the drinks are all bottled and freshly squeezed? No. I will never eat in this hotel again in my life.
In the morning, I went to have breakfast without any expectations and visit the old place. Ah! Much better than last night, a little richer. The hot dishes are steaming hot. A little bit of expectation. There are also more types of cakes, which are pretty good. As a result, I ate so much that I always wondered if I forgot to add salt, including cold dishes. I lost my appetite at noon. Whatâ€™s funny is that there is coffee in the evening and only milk and soy milk in the morning

name:Xâ€iâ€aâ€oâ€bâ€eâ€iâ€jâ€iâ€nâ€gâ€sâ€uâ€nâ€qâ€uâ€aâ€n

info:Stayed in November 2023

info:8 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted November 26, 2023
msg:Very satisfied with the stay.

In front of Wuyi Square, the transportation is convenient, the location is suitable, and it is relatively clean.

The bed, pillows and quilts are very comfortable, more comfortable than most international brand chains. The bathroom sink has good reviews and is very spacious.

The room is in the style of a traditional hotel. It is good except that there is no refrigerator. However, the window leaks a little and the sound insulation is a flaw of an old hotel.

The concierge service was very comfortable and attentive, and the fruits and small cakes given on the night of check-in were delicious.

If I have the chance to come to Taiyuan again, I will stay here again.

msg:The location is convenient, just at Wuyi Square, close to Willow Lane.
Parking is convenient, both ground and underground parking lots are available, and parking spaces are easy to find.
The decoration is exquisite and the facilities are very new.
The breakfast is rich, with dozens of varieties, and the dishes are updated every day. The fruits are delicious, as well as whole lamb soup, sliced â€‹â€‹noodles, and small fried dough sticks for state banquets are super delicious.
The water temperature in the swimming pool is 28 degrees, which is not cold at all.
The service was in place, and a beautiful cake was prepared for the child's birthday that day.

name:Aâ€nâ€oâ€nâ€yâ€mâ€oâ€uâ€sâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Business Standard Room (With view)
info:Stayed in May 2022
info:Other
info:35 Reviews
rating:4
posted:Posted May 15, 2022
msg:It can also be regarded as an old five-star hotel in Taiyuan. It is in Wuyi Square and has a great location. The parking lot is not big, just a place in front of the hotel. Entering the lobby, it is very spacious, and the check-in at the front desk is also very fast. This time we arranged room 1105 on the 11th floor. There is no need to swipe the room card to get on the elevator. This suggestion is improved, and I personally feel that it is not very safe. After going upstairs, the height of the corridor is very low. It may be like this in old hotels. I also encountered this problem when I stayed in Wanshi Jinghua some time ago. The room is not big, but enough. As a five-star hotel, there is no bathtub, which makes me wonder. The scenery in the room is really good. It is facing Wuyi Square, Bingzhou Hotel and Shanxi Hotel. It is beautiful no matter day or night. The welcome fruit sent by the hotel is quite considerate, as well as a pot of tea and two small cakes. Hotel slippers are a bit thinner than other five-star hotels. In terms of bedding, the bed is very soft and the pillows are just right, but the quilt is a little hard. I didn't eat breakfast, so I won't comment here. Also, the soundproofing of the room is really not very good. In general, as an old five-star hotel in Taiyuan, it has done a good job, but for friends who come to Taiyuan for the first time, I still recommend the Hubin International Hotel not far from it, where the scenery is better and the facilities are updated.
